+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import os
+import subprocess
+import sys
+from typing import Mapping, Sequence
+
+import hello
+import pytest
+
+
+def _run_module(
+    args: Sequence[str] | None = None, env: Mapping[str, str] | None = None
+) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess[str]:
+    """Invoke `python -m hello` and capture stdout/stderr for assertions."""
+    command = [sys.executable, "-m", "hello"]
+    if args:
+        command.extend(args)
+    merged_env = dict(os.environ)
+    if env:
+        merged_env.update(env)
+    return subprocess.run(  # noqa: S603,S607 subprocess usage intentional for CLI contract coverage
+        command,
+        capture_output=True,
+        text=True,
+        check=False,
+        env=merged_env if env else None,
+    )
+
+
+def test_fc_hello_greet_cap_1_sc_01_default_greeting() -> None:
+    """FC-HELLO-GREET-CAP-1-SC-01: default invocation prints Hello World once."""
+    result = _run_module()
+    expected_output = f"{hello.DEFAULT_MESSAGE}\n"
+    assert result.returncode == 0
+    assert result.stdout == expected_output
+    assert result.stderr == ""
+
+
+def test_fc_hello_greet_cap_1_sc_02_respects_env_toggle(
+    monkeypatch: pytest.MonkeyPatch,
+) -> None:
+    """FC-HELLO-GREET-CAP-1-SC-02: greeting remains stable when SYNTHETIC_RUN_LEVEL toggles."""
+    monkeypatch.setenv("SYNTHETIC_RUN_LEVEL", "spec")
+    result = _run_module(env={"SYNTHETIC_RUN_LEVEL": "spec"})
+    expected_output = f"{hello.DEFAULT_MESSAGE}\n"
+    assert result.returncode == 0
+    assert result.stdout == expected_output
+    assert result.stderr == ""
+
+
+def test_fc_hello_greet_cap_1_sc_03_rejects_unexpected_arguments() -> None:
+    """FC-HELLO-GREET-CAP-1-SC-03: unexpected positional arguments surface an argparse error."""
+    result = _run_module(["unexpected"])
+    assert result.returncode != 0
+    assert result.stdout == ""
+    assert "usage:" in result.stderr

### Runtime module (src/hello/__init__.py)

```python
from __future__ import annotations

import argparse
from collections.abc import Sequence

DEFAULT_MESSAGE = "Hello World"


def build_parser() -> argparse.ArgumentParser:
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Print a configurable greeting.")
    parser.add_argument(
        "--message",
        default=DEFAULT_MESSAGE,
        help="Override the greeting message.",
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "--repeat",
        type=int,
        default=1,
        help="Number of times to print the greeting.",
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "--quiet",
        action="store_true",
        help="Suppress output.",
    )
    return parser


def main(argv: Sequence[str] | None = None) -> int:
    parser = build_parser()
    args = parser.parse_args(argv)
    repeats = args.repeat if args.repeat >= 0 else 0
    if not args.quiet and repeats > 0:
        for _ in range(repeats):
            print(args.message)
    return 0


def run() -> int:
    return main(None)
```
### CLI entry (src/hello/__main__.py)

```python
from __future__ import annotations

from . import main


def entrypoint() -> int:
    return main(None)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    raise SystemExit(entrypoint())
```
